  <calculation name="10.tdb" type="section" duration="2.3" original_batch_name="" id="0"> 
    <databases>
      <database type="tdb" file_name="10.tdb" />
    </databases>
    <units>
      <unit name="P" value="bar" />
      <unit name="T" value="K" />
      <unit name="n" value="x" />
    </units>
    <system name="Default_System">
      <components>
        <component name="Ag" status="Selected" />
        <component name="Sn" status="Selected" />
      </components>
      <phases>
        <phase name="*" status="Entered" />
      </phases>
      <points>
        <point>
          <statespace>
            <T value="2300" />
            <P value="1" />
            <n component="Ag" value="1" />
            <n component="Sn" value="0" />
          </statespace>
        </point>
        <point>
          <statespace>
            <T value="300" />
            <P value="1" />
            <n component="Ag" value="1" />
            <n component="Sn" value="0" />
          </statespace>
        </point>
        <point>
          <statespace>
            <T value="300" />
            <P value="1" />
            <n component="Ag" value="0" />
            <n component="Sn" value="1" />
          </statespace>
        </point>
      </points>
      <condition>
      </condition>
    </system>
    <output unit="">
      <tables>
        <table name="10.tdb" source="invariant" type="invariant">
          <column name="T" />
          <column name="reaction" />
          <column name="phase_name" />
          <column name="#phases" />
          <column name="x(*)" />
          <column name="w(*)" />
          <column name="f(@*)" />
        </table>
      </tables>
    </output>
  </calculation>
